<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отгородить.html>отгороди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otgorodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отгородиться.html>отгороди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otgorodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отгораживаться.html>отгора́живаться</a></b>)

***отдавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдавать.html>отдава́ть</a> (1601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдавать.html>отдава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдать.html>отда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give back, to return</li>
<li>to give (away), to hand over, to give up, to give over</li>
<li>to send
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отдавать.html>отдава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́лу</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdavátʹ</b> rebjónka v škólu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to send a child to school</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to devote</li>
<li>to cast (anchor)</li>
<li>to recoil (of a gun)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаваться.html>отдава́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otdavátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаться.html>отда́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otdátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***отдаваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдаваться.html>отдава́ться</a> (8362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдавать.html>отдава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаваться.html>отдава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdavátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаться.html>отда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give oneself up <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаваться.html>отдава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdavátʹsja</b> na mílostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw oneself in the mercy (of)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to surrender oneself <i>(to)</i>, to give oneself up <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to yield <i>(to)</i>, to put out <i>(to)</i> <i>(have sex)</i></li>
<li>to resound, to reverberate, to ring</li>
<li>to make
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаваться.html>отдава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́лью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdavátʹsja</b> bólʹju v sérdce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make one's heart bleed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёзы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдаться.html>отдались</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалость.html>жа́лостью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jejó sljózy otdalisʹ vo mne žálostʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">her tears made me feel sorry for her</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдавать.html>отдава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***отдалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдалить.html>отдали́ть</a> (7226)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дали́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдалить.html>отдали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отдаля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hold away, to move away</li>
<li>to postpone, to put off</li>
<li>to estrange, to alienate</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отдаля́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li>to drift apart, to become estranged
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постепенно.html>постепе́нно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаляться.html>отдаля́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní postepénno <b>otdaljálisʹ</b> drug ot drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they gradually drifted apart</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***отдать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдать.html>отда́ть</a> (711)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдать.html>отда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдавать.html>отдава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give back, to return</li>
<li>to give (away), to hand over, to give up, to give over</li>
<li>to send</li>
<li>to devote</li>
<li>to cast (anchor)</li>
<li>to recoil (of a gun)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдаться.html>отда́ться</a> (11887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдать.html>отда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаться.html>отда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаваться.html>отдава́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give oneself up <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отдаться.html>отда́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdátʹsja</b> na mílostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw oneself in the mercy (of)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to surrender oneself <i>(to)</i>, to give oneself up <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to yield <i>(to)</i>, to put out <i>(to)</i> <i>(have sex)</i></li>
<li>to resound, to reverberate, to ring</li>
<li>to make
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">отдавься <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́лью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdavʹsja bólʹju v sérdce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make one's heart bleed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёзы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдаться.html>отдались</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалость.html>жа́лостью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jejó sljózy otdalisʹ vo mne žálostʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">her tears made me feel sorry for her</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдать.html>отда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***отдача.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́ча</a> (12673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdáča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>return
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez otdáči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for good</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́чи</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vzjatʹ bez <b>otdáči</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">take without the intention of giving back; take for keeps</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> recoil, kick
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́ча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рулевой.html>рулево́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колонок.html>колонки́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdáča rulevój kolonki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">steering kickback</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>efficiency, output
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́чей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s pólnoj otdáčej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wholeheartedly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́ча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инвестиция.html>инвести́ций</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdáča investícij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">return on investment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́ча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:емкость.html>ёмкости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdáča po jómkosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">capacity efficiency</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́ча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пласт.html>пласта́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdáča plastá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">productive capacity of the reservoir</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">naval</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dropping, casting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отдача.html>отда́ча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:якорь.html>якоря</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdáča</b> jakorja</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">dropping/casting of the anchor</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***отделать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a> (12127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdélatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отде́лывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to finish, to trim <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ру</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdélatʹ</b> kvartíru</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to decorate a flat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to trim <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тье</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кружево.html>кружева́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdélatʹ</b> plátʹje kruževámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to trim a dress with lace</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spoil, to ruin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat, to wallop, to lick, to give the works, to give the business, to tan someone's hide</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лка</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otdélka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отде́лочный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otdéločnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otdélyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otdélatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***отделаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a> (6470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdélatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdélatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get rid <i>(of)</i>, to get away <i>(from)</i>, to throw off, to shake off, to be through <i>(with)</i>, to finish <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne mogú <b>otdélatʹsja</b> ot vpečatlénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I can't shake off [get away from] the impression</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to escape <i>(with)</i>, to get away <i>(with)</i>, to get off <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фраза.html>фра́зами</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdélatʹsja</b> óbščimi frázami (ot)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to talk one's way out (of)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отговорка.html>отгово́рками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdélatʹsja</b> otgovórkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get away with excuses; get away with irrelevant comments; dodge the question; give the runaround</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get away <i>(with)</i>, to get off <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:царапина.html>цара́пинами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdélatʹsja</b> carápinami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get off/away with slight cuts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дёшево</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">djóševo <b>otdélatʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get off easy/cheap</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>сча́стливо</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>счастли́во</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sčástlivo/sčastlívo <b>otdélatʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a lucky escape; be none the worse for it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdélatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***отделивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделивший.html>отдели́вший</a> (9560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделить.html>отдели́ть</a> (9560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделить.html>отдели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdelítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделять.html>отделя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to separate, to detach, to part</li>
<li>to disjoint, to divorce, to separate off</li>
<li>to divide, to serve as boundary</li>
<li>to secrete</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лка</a> (20144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdélatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to finish, to trim</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdélka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>finishing, trimming, decoration work/finish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окончательный.html>оконча́тельная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">okončátelʹnaja <b>otdélka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">finishing touches</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">чистовая <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čistovaja <b>otdélka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">smoothing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>finish, decoration, trimmings
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружевной.html>кружевна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kruževnája <b>otdélka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">lace trimmings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внутренний.html>вну́тренняя</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделка.html>отде́лка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vnútrennjaja <b>otdélka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">interior decoration</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***отделываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a> (32173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отде́лывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdélyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdélyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get rid <i>(of)</i>, to get away <i>(from)</i>, to throw off, to shake off, to be through <i>(with)</i>, to finish <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne mogú <b>otdélyvatʹsja</b> ot vpečatlénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I can't shake off [get away from] the impression</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to escape <i>(with)</i>, to get away <i>(with)</i>, to get off <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фраза.html>фра́зами</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdélyvatʹsja</b> óbščimi frázami (ot)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to talk one's way out (of)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отговорка.html>отгово́рками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdélyvatʹsja</b> otgovórkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get away with excuses; get away with irrelevant comments; dodge the question; give the runaround</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get away <i>(with)</i>, to get off <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:царапина.html>цара́пинами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otdélyvatʹsja</b> carápinami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get off/away with slight cuts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дёшево</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">djóševo <b>otdélyvatʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get off easy/cheap</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>сча́стливо</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>счастли́во</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отделываться.html>отде́лываться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sčástlivo/sčastlívo <b>otdélyvatʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a lucky escape; be none the worse for it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отде́лывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdélyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
